 thode din baad jab gaanv gaya to suna ki kal shaam koi masterji bank se tankhwaah lekar ghar ja rahe the, badmaashon ne paise bhi chin liye or motorcycle bhi

 Rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh, the world's largest voluntary organization, was founded by Keshav Balaram Hedgewar
 bharat ko hindu raashtra banane ke lakshya ke saath 27 sitambar 1925 ko vijaydashami ke din aresas kii sthapana kii gai thi

 nagpur ke akhaadon se taiyaar hua sangh maujuuda samay main viraat rup le chukaa he
 Started by less than two dozen people, Hedgewar, the first Sarsanghchalak of the Sangh, planned to form the Sangh in a seminar with 17 people at his home
 is baithak main headgavar ke saath vishwanath kelkar, bhauji kaaware, anna saahane, balaji huddaar, baapuro bhedi aadi maujuud the

 us vakt hinduon ko sirf sangathit karne kaa vichaar tha
 Even the RSS was christened 'rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh' on 17 April 1926
 isi din headgavar ko sarvasammati se sangh pramukh chunaa gaya, lekin sarasanghachaalak ve november 1929 main banaae gaye
 Such was the name RSS National self-service Association, this name was brainstormed before coming into existence
 rashtriya swayamsevak sangh, jaripatka mandal or bharatodwarak mandal in teen naamon par vichaar hua

 swasth or sugathit swayamsevak hona unki kalpana main tha

 sangh parivaar main 80 se zyada samavichaari yaa anushangik sanghathan hai
 The association is active in about 40 countries of the world
 maujuuda samay main sangh kii 56 hajaar 569 dainik shakhaaen lagati hai
 There are also about 13 thousand 847 weekly congregations and 9 thousand monthly branches
 sangh main sadasyon kaa panjikaran nahin hota
 Based on the presence of such branches, it is estimated that currently more than 50 lakh volunteers regularly visit the branches
 desh kii har tehsil or kareeb 55 hajaar gaanvon main shakha lag rahi he
 Sanctioned three times The Sangh made many achievements in its long journey, while it was banned three times

 isse prabhavit hokar pradhanmantri nehru ne 1963 main ganatantr diwas kii parade main sangh ko bulaayaa tha
